        //标签筛选
        function switchMetro(flag) {
            $(".tagfilter_metro").removeClass("xzbold");
            $("#" + flag).addClass("xzbold");
            $("#" + flag).parents('.newlist_list1').addClass('newlist_list1_zk');
            $("#" + flag).parents('.newlist_list1').removeClass('newlist_list1');
            $(".tagfilter_metrostation").hide();
            $("." + flag).show();
        }

		function switchTag(url) {
			var currUrl = $("#MetroStationCurrUrl").val();
			window.location = currUrl+url;
        }

		$(document).ready(function () {			
            //地铁折叠
            var metroOpen = $.cookie('metroopen');
            if (metroOpen == "1") {
                $('.newlist_metro').show();
                $('#metroswitch').removeClass("newlist_metroswitchup").addClass("newlist_metroswitchdown");
            } else {
                $('.newlist_metro').hide();
                $('#metroswitch').removeClass("newlist_metroswitchdown").addClass("newlist_metroswitchup");
            }
            $('#metroswitch').click(function () {
                var metroDisplay = $('.newlist_metro').css("display");
                if (metroDisplay == "none") {
                    $.cookie('metroopen', '1', { expires: 30, path: '/' });
                    $('.newlist_metro').slideDown(500);
                    $(this).removeClass("newlist_metroswitchup").addClass("newlist_metroswitchdown");
                } else {
                    $.cookie('metroopen', '0', { expires: 30, path: '/' });
                    if ($('#c23').val() == "") {
                        $('.newlist_metro').slideUp(500);
                        $(this).removeClass("newlist_metroswitchdown").addClass("newlist_metroswitchup");
                    }
                    else {
                        location.href = $("#nometro").attr("href");
                    }
                }
            });
            //职位类别折叠
            var jobtype_tag = $("#search_jobtype_tag");
            if (jobtype_tag.length > 0) {
                var jobtypeOpen = $.cookie('jobtypeopen');
                var height = jobtype_tag.css("height").replace("px", "");
                if (height > 68) {
                    $("#search_jobtype_tag").next().show();
                    if (jobtypeOpen == "0" || $('#c6').val() == "")
                        $("#search_jobtype_tag").css("height", "68px");
                }
                else {
                    $("#search_jobtype_tag").next().hide();
                }
            }
            $('#jobtypeswitch').click(function () {
                var height = $("#search_jobtype_tag").css("height").replace("px", "");
                if (height == 68) {
                    $.cookie('jobtypeopen', '1', { expires: 30, path: '/' });
                    $("#search_jobtype_tag").css("height", "auto");
                } else {
                    $.cookie('jobtypeopen', '0', { expires: 30, path: '/' });
                    $("#search_jobtype_tag").css("height", "68px");
                }
            });
        })
    </script>

<script type="text/javascript">
    //   验证码校验
    var ajaxVlidate;
    function validate_indent_code(errorFun, succFun) {
        var indentCode = $("#ident_code");
        var result = false;
        if (indentCode.val().replace(/^\s|\s$/g, "") != "") {
            var url = '/Assist/SubscibeWithNotLogin?operate=checkcode';
            var params = $('#formSubscibe').serialize();
            validate_indent = $.ajax({
                url: url,
                type: 'post',
                async: false,
                data: params,
                success: function (result) {
                    var jsonResult = result;
                    var status = false;
                    if (jsonResult.Status < 0) {
                        if (jsonResult.Description == "验证码错误") {
                            indentCode.parent().get(0).className = 'inputText1 span_input inputTexte_indent';
                            $("#randomNews_indent").html("验证码错误");
                            ident_image_load();
                            if (errorFun && errorFun instanceof Function) {
                                errorFun();
                            }
                        }
                    } else if (jsonResult.Status >= 0) {
                        indentCode.parent().get(0).className = 'inputText1 span_input inputTexts_indent';
                        $("#randomNews_indent").html("");
                        if (succFun && succFun instanceof Function) {
                            succFun();
                        }
                    }
                }
            });
        } else {
            indentCode.parent().get(0).className = 'inputText1 span_input inputTexte_indent';
            $("#randomNews_indent").html("请输入验证码");
            if (errorFun && errorFun instanceof Function) {
                errorFun();
            }
        }
    }
    //  验证码重加载
    function ident_image_load() {
        var identDom = $('.ident_image').get(0);
        var timeTamp = +new Date().getTime();
        identDom.src = "/Assist/GetCaptcha?timeTamp=" + timeTamp;
    }
    //  loading状态开始
    function beg_send_free_book_job() {

        if (emailTemp && emailTemp.checkData($("#email").get(0)) == "0") {
            $(".input_submit").attr({ onclick: "" })
            $(".submit_waiting").show();
            return true;
        } else {
            if ($("#email").val() == "") {
                $("#email").get(0).onblur();
            }
            return false;
        }
    }
    //  loading状态结束并且 一秒后关闭弹层
    function end_send_free_book_job() {
        $(".input_submit").html("订阅成功");
        setTimeout(function () {
            $("#id_job_read_container").hide();
        }, 1000);
    }
    //  form提交方法
    function subscibe() {
        var url = '/Assist/SubscibeWithNotLogin';
        //邮件校验
        if (ajaxVlidate) {
            ajaxVlidate.abort();
        }
        ajaxVlidate = null;
        if (!beg_send_free_book_job()) {
            return false;
        }
        $(".input_submit").unbind('click');
        //验证码校验
        validate_indent_code(function () {
            $(".input_submit").bind('click', subscibe);
            // $(".input_submit").attr({ onclick: "subscibe();" });
            $(".submit_waiting").hide();
        }, function () {
            var params = $('#formSubscibe').serialize();
            $.ajax({
                url: url,
                type: 'post',
                data: params,
                success: function (result) {
                    var jsonResult = result;
                    $(".submit_waiting").hide();
                    if (jsonResult.Status < 0) {
                        //$(".input_submit").attr({ onclick: "subscibe();" });
                        $(".input_submit").bind('click', subscibe);
                        if (jsonResult.Description == "验证码错误") {
                            indentCode.parent().get(0).className = 'inputText1 span_input inputTexte_indent';
                            $("#randomNews_indent").html("验证码错误");
                        } else {
                            //  其它错误
                        }
                        $(".submit_waiting").hide();
                    } else if (jsonResult.Status >= 0) {
                        end_send_free_book_job();
                        ident_image_load();
                    }
                }
            });
        });
    }
</script>    <a class="search_cztj" href="/jobs/searchresult.ashx">

<script src="/assets/javascript/jquery.json.js"></script>
<script type="text/javascript">
    var count = $('.search_yx_tj').find('em').text();
    var url4zpAnalytics = document.location.pathname + document.location.search + '&rt=' + count;
    var CurrentSearchHistory = {
        "Name": "php + 成都",
        "SearchUrl": "http://sou.zhaopin.com/jobs/searchresult.ashx?jl=%e6%88%90%e9%83%bd&amp;kw=PHP&amp;sm=0&amp;p=1"
    }
    $(document).ready(function () {
        renderSearchHistory();
        $(".search_yb").unbind().click(function () {
            saveSearchHistory(CurrentSearchHistory.Name, CurrentSearchHistory.SearchUrl);
        });
    });

    function saveSearchHistory(name, url) {
        try {
            var searchHistorysCookie = $.cookie('SearchHistory');
            var searchHistorys;
            if (searchHistorysCookie) {
                searchHistorys = $.evalJSON(searchHistorysCookie);
                if (searchHistorys.length == 3) {
                    searchHistorys.pop();
                }
                searchHistorys.unshift({
                    "Name": name,
                    "SearchUrl": url
                });
            } else {
                searchHistorys = [
                    {
                        "Name": name,
                        "SearchUrl": url
                    }
                ];
            }
            $.cookie('SearchHistory', $.toJSON(searchHistorys), { expires: 30, path: '/' });
            renderSearchHistory();
            saveSearchHistoryOver();
        } catch (ex) { }
    }

    function renderSearchHistory() {
        try {
            var searchHistorysCookie = $.cookie('SearchHistory');
            if (searchHistorysCookie) {
                var searchHistorys = $.evalJSON(searchHistorysCookie);
                $("#SearchHistoryCount").html(searchHistorys.length);
                if (searchHistorys.length > 0) {
                    var sb = [];
                    for (var i = 0; i < searchHistorys.length; i++) {
                        var searchHistory = searchHistorys[i];
                        sb.push('<li class="clearfix"><a href="' + searchHistory.SearchUrl + '">' + searchHistory.Name + '</a><span onClick="javascript:deleteSearchHistory(' + i + ');"></span></li>');
                    }
                    $("#SearchHistoryList")[0].innerHTML = sb.join("");
                } else {
                    $("#SearchHistoryList")[0].innerHTML = "";
                    $(".search_yb").removeClass("saveover").css("color", "#3359ac").unbind().click(function () {
                        saveSearchHistory(CurrentSearchHistory.Name, CurrentSearchHistory.SearchUrl);
                    });
                }
            } else {
                $("#SearchHistoryCount").html("0");
            }
        } catch (ex) { }
    }

    function deleteSearchHistory(index) {
        try {
            var searchHistorysCookie = $.cookie('SearchHistory');
            if (searchHistorysCookie) {
                var searchHistorys = $.evalJSON(searchHistorysCookie);
                if (searchHistorys.length >= index + 1) {
                    searchHistorys.splice(index, 1);
                }
                $.cookie('SearchHistory', $.toJSON(searchHistorys), { expires: 30, path: '/' });
            }
            renderSearchHistory();
        }
        catch (ex) { }
    }

    function saveSearchHistoryOver() {
        if (!$(".search_yb").hasClass("saveover")) {
            $(".search_yb").addClass("saveover").css("color", "#999").unbind();
            $('.relucss_tc').stop().fadeIn();
            setTimeout(function () {
                $('.relucss_tc').stop().fadeOut();
            }, 1000);
        }
    }
</script>

    /*排除公司*/
    $(document).ready(function () {
        $(".del_company").click( //点击排除公司显示弹层
            function () {
                var jqalertbox = $(".alert_box").get(0);
                /*var oDiv = document.getElementById('div_01');
                var jqalertbox_top = parseInt(oDiv.style.top) - $(".alert_box").height() + 63
                jqalertbox.style.top = parseInt(jqalertbox_top) + 'px';*/
                if ($(".alert_box")[0].style.display == "none") {
                    $(".alert_box").show();
                    if (unit_layer != undefined) {
                        unit_layer.init_remove_comps();
                    }
                    //  监控事件触发
                    dyweTrackEvent('forbidcompwithsou', 'showfcdiv');
                }
            });
        $(".alt_close01").click( //关闭弹层
            function () {
                //  监控事件触发
                $(".alert_box").hide();
                dyweTrackEvent('forbidcompwithsou', 'cancelfc');
            });
    });
</script>

		$(document).ready(function () {
			var vas = document.getElementsByName("vacancyid");			
			if (vas != null) {			
				var vacancyids="";
				$("input:[name='vacancyid']").each(function () {
					vacancyids+=$(this).val()+",";
				});
				if (vacancyids == "") {
					//用基础方法获取
					for (var i = 0; i < vas.length; i++) {
						vacancyids += vas[i].getAttribute("value")+",";
					}
				}				
				dyweTrackEventExpo('jobs', 'expo', vacancyids);
            }
        });
    </script>

    <script type="text/javascript">
        $(document).ready(function () {
            $(window).bind("scroll resize load", function () {
                var bodyScrollTop = $(window).scrollTop();
                if (bodyScrollTop == 0) {
                    $("#go_top_layer").hide();
                } else {
                    $("#go_top_layer").show();
                }
            });
            $(".back_top").click(//定义返回顶部点击向上滚动的动画
                function () {
                    $('html,body').animate({ scrollTop: 0 }, 300);
                });
        });
    </script>

    function loadScript(url, callback) {
        var script = document.createElement("script")
        script.type = "text/javascript";
        if (script.readyState) {
            script.onreadystatechange = function () {
                if (script.readyState == "loaded" || script.readyState == "complete") {
                    script.onreadystatechange = null;
                    callback();
                }
            };
        } else {
            script.onload = function () {
                callback();
            };
        }
        script.src = url;
        var s = document.getElementsByTagName("script")[0];
        s.parentNode.insertBefore(script, s);
    }
